var snhb = snhb || {}; snhb.queue = snhb.queue || [];

function nbc_pagecall() {
  // get and set pagecall cookie
  var cookie = document.cookie.split(";");
  var call = 0;
  for(var i=0; i<cookie.length; i++) {
    var c = cookie[i];
    while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
    if (c.indexOf("nbc_call=") == 0) call = c.substring(9,c.length);
  }
  call = parseInt(call);
  call++;
  if (call>2) call=3; // only 1, 2 or 3 as options
  // set custom targeting for dfp
  googletag.cmd.push(function() {googletag.pubads().setTargeting("pagecall", String(call));});
  // save cookie
  var expires = new Date();
  var days = 1;
  expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));
  document.cookie="nbc_call="+call+";expires="+expires.toUTCString()+";path=/";
  console.log("pagecall set to "+call);
}

   function toggleMe(a){ 
var e=document.getElementById(a);  
if(e.style.display=="none" || e.style.maxHeight!=""){ 
 e.style.display="block";
 e.style.maxHeight="";
 if (document.getElementById(a+"_a1")) document.getElementById(a+"_a1").style.display="none";
 if (document.getElementById(a+"_a2")) document.getElementById(a+"_a2").style.display="";
 if (document.getElementById(a+"_gr")) document.getElementById(a+"_gr").style.display="none";
} else { 
 e.style.display="none";
 if (document.getElementById(a+"_a1")) document.getElementById(a+"_a1").style.display="";
 if (document.getElementById(a+"_a2")) document.getElementById(a+"_a2").style.display="none";
 if (document.getElementById(a+"_gr")) document.getElementById(a+"_gr").style.display="";
} 
return false;}

function convertTime(utctimetoconvert) {
	userDate = new Date();
	var utcTime = userDate.getTime();
	utcTime = Math.round(utcTime/1000);
	timeDiff = utcTime-utctimetoconvert;
	if (timeDiff<0) result_str = "";
	else {
		var days = Math.floor(timeDiff / (60 * 60 * 24));
		timeDiff -=  days * (60 * 60 * 24);

		var hours = Math.floor(timeDiff / (60 * 60));
		timeDiff -= hours * (60 * 60);

		var mins = Math.floor(timeDiff / (60));
		timeDiff -= mins * (60);

		var seconds = Math.floor(timeDiff) ;
		timeDiff -= seconds;

		var result_str = "";
		if (days>0) {
			if (days==1) result_str = days + " day";
			else result_str = days + " days";
		}
		if (days<2) {
			if (result_str && hours>0) result_str += ", ";
			if (hours>0) {
				if (hours==1) result_str += hours + " hour";
				else result_str += hours + " hours";
			}
			if (result_str && mins>0) result_str += ", ";
			if (mins>0 && days<1) {
				if (mins==1) result_str += mins + " minute";
				else result_str += mins + " minutes";
			}
			if (days==0 && hours==0 && mins<5) {
				if (result_str && seconds>0) result_str += ", ";
				if (seconds>0) {
					if (seconds==1) result_str += seconds + " second";
					else result_str += seconds + " seconds";
				}
			}
		}
		result_str = " "+result_str+" ago";
	}
	var x = document.getElementsByClassName("itemdate_"+utctimetoconvert);
	var i;
	for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
			x[i].innerHTML = result_str;
	}
}

         <div class="introa_whole">
          <script type="text/javascript">
           var loading_1250525 = false; // loading indicator;
				var loading_num_1250525 = 0; // incrementing loading num;			
						
				jQuery(document).ready(function() {		
					//jQuery("img").unveil(200);

					
					
					/*
					jQuery(".introa_rl_hoverable").hover(function() {
						jQuery(this).children().children(".introa_rl_box").slideToggle(400); // if more than one element is on the page, this is attached more than once for each element
					});
					*/
					
										
					// hide settings (do it in javascript, to show it to browsers without javascript enabled)
					//jQuery(".introa_form").slideUp(100);
				});

				function ajaxReload_1250525(tt_content_uid,page,items_per_page,no_url_change) {
				
					if (loading_1250525==true) { // do not call if already loading
						//jQuery("#introa_loading_info_1250525").html("already loading ...");
						//return false;
					}
					
					loading_1250525 = true;
					
					items_per_page = typeof items_per_page !== "undefined" ? items_per_page : 50;
					
					jQuery("#introa_ajax_"+tt_content_uid).html("loading ...");
					jQuery("#introa_ajax_"+tt_content_uid).show();
					jQuery("#introa_loading_info_"+tt_content_uid).html("loading ...");
					//console.log("loading "+items_per_page+" elements ...");
					jQuery("#introa_loading_info_"+tt_content_uid).show();
					if (jQuery("#introa_content_"+tt_content_uid).length) jQuery("#introa_content_"+tt_content_uid).fadeTo( 250, 0.2);

					// set default to 0 for the page
					page = typeof page !== "undefined" ? page : 0;
					
					
					
					var tagArray = new Array();
					
					// get checkbox value for the tags
					container = document.getElementById("introa_cbox_tag_surround_"+tt_content_uid); // get container div of the checkboxes
					if (container) {
						inputs = container.getElementsByTagName("input"); // get all input fields in the images div
						for (index = 0; index < inputs.length; ++index) {
							if(inputs[index].checked) tagArray.push(inputs[index].value);
						} // for
					} // if container
					
					var typeArray = new Array();
					
					// get checkbox value for the pagetypes
					container = document.getElementById("introa_cbox_type_surround_"+tt_content_uid); // get container div of the checkboxes
					if (container) {
						inputs = container.getElementsByTagName("input"); // get all input fields in the images div
						for (index = 0; index < inputs.length; ++index) {
							if(inputs[index].checked) typeArray.push(inputs[index].value);
						} // for
					} // if container

					loading_num_1250525++;

					var paraArray = {"id":98933,"ns_ajax":1,"language":2
						,"loading_num":loading_num_1250525,"ns_json":1
						,"ns_tt_content_uid":1250525}; 
					/*"ns_page_uid":48,*/
					if (items_per_page != 50) paraArray.items_per_page=items_per_page
					if(document.getElementById("introa_cbox_ticker_"+tt_content_uid).checked) paraArray.ticker=1;
					if(document.getElementById("introa_cbox_tag_or_"+tt_content_uid).checked) paraArray.tag_or=1;
					if (1>0) paraArray.hide_date=1;
					if (0>0) paraArray.ns_hide_restrictions=0;
					if (0>0) paraArray.ns_layout=0;
					if (1>0) paraArray.hide_youtube=1;
					if (0>0) paraArray.order_by_sorting=0;
					if (0>0) paraArray.ns_show_hr=0;
					if (0>0) paraArray.ns_featured_articles_only=0;
					if (0>0) paraArray.ns_hide_navigation_buttons=0;
					if (0>0) paraArray.ns_show_num_normal=0;
					if (0>0) paraArray.hide_external_reviews=0;
					if (0>0) paraArray.ns_article_pid=0;
					if ("") paraArray.ns_img_domain="";
					if (0>0) paraArray.clear_news_stream_image_caches=1;
					
					if (tagArray.length>0) paraArray.tagArray=tagArray;
					if (typeArray.length>0) paraArray.typeArray=typeArray;
					if (page>0) paraArray.page=page;
					var title = jQuery("#introa_search_title_"+tt_content_uid).val();
					if (title) paraArray.introa_search_title=title;

					jQuery("#introa_ajax_"+tt_content_uid).show();
					
					
					jQuery.ajax({url: "//dev1.notebook-check.com/index.php",type: "GET",
						/* url: "index.php", */
						data: paraArray
						})
						.done(function(data) {
							jQuery("#introa_currently_loaded_1250525").html(items_per_page);

							// move google ads
							//jQuery("#introa_googleads_1250525").appendTo("#introa_googleads_temp_1250525"); // problem - iframe ads are shown too large after moving!
							
							try {
								obj = JSON.parse(data);
							}	catch(e){
								console.log(e); //error in the above string(in this case,yes)!
							}
							
							if (obj.loading_num != loading_num_1250525) {
								console.log("discarded loading #"+obj.loading_num+" as a newer request #"+loading_num_1250525+" is under way");
								return 0;
							}
							

							jQuery("#introa_ajax_"+tt_content_uid).html("");
							jQuery("#introa_ajax_"+tt_content_uid).hide();
							jQuery("#introa_content_"+tt_content_uid).html(obj.data);
							jQuery("#introa_loading_info_"+tt_content_uid).hide();
							if (jQuery("#introa_content_"+tt_content_uid).length) jQuery("#introa_content_"+tt_content_uid).fadeTo( 250, 1);
							
							// add hover for the new elements
							/*
							jQuery(".introa_rl_hoverable").hover(function() {
								jQuery(this).children().children(".introa_rl_box").slideToggle(400);
							});
							*/	
							// get query string with parameters (ignore ajax parameters)
							var queryString = "";
							for (var key in paraArray) {
								if (key != "id" && key != "ns_ajax" && key != "language" 
										&& key != "tagArray[]" && key != "tagArray"
										&& key != "typeArray[]" && key != "typeArray"
										&& key != "loading_num" && key != "ns_json" 
										&& key != "ns_page_uid" && key != "ns_tt_content_uid") {
									if (paraArray[key])	queryString += "&"+key+"="+paraArray[key];
								}
							}
							for (var key in tagArray) { // add tagArray
								if (tagArray[key]>0) queryString += "&tagArray[]="+tagArray[key];
							}
							for (var key in typeArray) { // add typeArray
								if (typeArray[key]>0) queryString += "&typeArray[]="+typeArray[key];
							}
							// change url
							var stateObj = { foo: "bar" };
							history.pushState(stateObj, "", "?"+queryString);
							
							// rebind unveil to dynamically load images
							//jQuery("img").unveil(200);

							loading = false;

						})
						.fail(function(data) {
							jQuery("#introa_ajax_1250525").html("loading failed!");
							jQuery("#introa_loading_info_1250525").html("loading failed!");
							loading = false;
						});

function convertTime(utctimetoconvert) {
	userDate = new Date();
	var utcTime = userDate.getTime();
	utcTime = Math.round(utcTime/1000);
	timeDiff = utcTime-utctimetoconvert;
	if (timeDiff<0) result_str = "";
	else {
		var days = Math.floor(timeDiff / (60 * 60 * 24));
		timeDiff -=  days * (60 * 60 * 24);

		var hours = Math.floor(timeDiff / (60 * 60));
		timeDiff -= hours * (60 * 60);

		var mins = Math.floor(timeDiff / (60));
		timeDiff -= mins * (60);

		var seconds = Math.floor(timeDiff) ;
		timeDiff -= seconds;

		var result_str = "";
		if (days>0) {
			if (days==1) result_str = days + " day";
			else result_str = days + " days";
		}
		if (days<2) {
			if (result_str && hours>0) result_str += ", ";
			if (hours>0) {
				if (hours==1) result_str += hours + " hour";
				else result_str += hours + " hours";
			}
			if (result_str && mins>0) result_str += ", ";
			if (mins>0 && days<1) {
				if (mins==1) result_str += mins + " minute";
				else result_str += mins + " minutes";
			}
			if (days==0 && hours==0 && mins<5) {
				if (result_str && seconds>0) result_str += ", ";
				if (seconds>0) {
					if (seconds==1) result_str += seconds + " second";
					else result_str += seconds + " seconds";
				}
			}
		}
		result_str = " "+result_str+" ago";
	}
	var x = document.getElementsByClassName("itemdate_"+utctimetoconvert);
	var i;
	for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
			x[i].innerHTML = result_str;
	}
}

						} // for

					loading_num_1++;

					var paraArray = {"id":98933,"ns_ajax":1,"language":2

function convertTime(utctimetoconvert) {
	userDate = new Date();
	var utcTime = userDate.getTime();
	utcTime = Math.round(utcTime/1000);
	timeDiff = utcTime-utctimetoconvert;
	if (timeDiff<0) result_str = "";
	else {
		var days = Math.floor(timeDiff / (60 * 60 * 24));
		timeDiff -=  days * (60 * 60 * 24);

		var hours = Math.floor(timeDiff / (60 * 60));
		timeDiff -= hours * (60 * 60);

		var mins = Math.floor(timeDiff / (60));
		timeDiff -= mins * (60);

		var seconds = Math.floor(timeDiff) ;
		timeDiff -= seconds;

		var result_str = "";
		if (days>0) {
			if (days==1) result_str = days + " day";
			else result_str = days + " days";
		}
		if (days<2) {
			if (result_str && hours>0) result_str += ", ";
			if (hours>0) {
				if (hours==1) result_str += hours + " hour";
				else result_str += hours + " hours";
			}
			if (result_str && mins>0) result_str += ", ";
			if (mins>0 && days<1) {
				if (mins==1) result_str += mins + " minute";
				else result_str += mins + " minutes";
			}
			if (days==0 && hours==0 && mins<5) {
				if (result_str && seconds>0) result_str += ", ";
				if (seconds>0) {
					if (seconds==1) result_str += seconds + " second";
					else result_str += seconds + " seconds";
				}
			}
		}
		result_str = " "+result_str+" ago";
	}
	var x = document.getElementsByClassName("itemdate_"+utctimetoconvert);
	var i;
	for (i = 0; i < x.length; i++) {
			x[i].innerHTML = result_str;
	}
}
            </script>

       <h2>
        About us
       </h2>
       <h1 style="font-size:13px; font-weight:bold; font-family:Arial; text-shadow:none; letter-spacing:normal;">
        Laptop, Tablet and Smartphone Reviews, Tech, and News
       </h1>
       Our aim is to provide serious and competent information about notebooks,
smartphones and tablets. For more than 16 years now, Notebookcheck has provided detailed
       <a href="Reviews.55.0.html">
        tests, reviews
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="News.152.0.html">
        news
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="Benchmarks-Tech.123.0.html">
        technical information
       </a>
       (like our
       <a href="Mobile-Processors-Benchmark-List.2436.0.html">
        CPU
       </a>
       and
       <a href="Mobile-Graphics-Cards-Benchmark-List.844.0.html">
        GPU benchmarks
       </a>
       )
and
       <a href="Library.279.0.html">
        links to reviews by other sites
       </a>
       .
